## **CASE OVERVIEW**
**Defendant:** Live-in caregiver providing disability accommodation services  
**Jurisdiction:** Stanislaus County, California  
**Case Type:** Unlawful Detainer (Eviction)  
**Filing Deadline:** 8AM court appearance  

---

## **‚ö° ATTACK VECTOR #1: SERVICE OF PROCESS VIOLATIONS**

**CRITICAL FACTS:**
- June 20th: Substitute service filed
- Today: Landlord NOW claiming "personal service" for judgment
- **SMOKING GUN:** Direct contradiction in service type claims
- **MISSING:** Required certified mail for substitute service
- **MISSING:** Proof of service filing with court

**LEGAL VIOLATIONS:**
- CCP 415.20(b): Incomplete substitute service
- CCP 1162: UD-specific service requirements  
- CCP 417.10: Proof of service filing requirement
- **PERJURY:** False sworn statements about service type

**DEFENSE STRATEGY:** Motion to Set Aside Default - Void service = Void judgment

---

## **‚ö° ATTACK VECTOR #2: 1946.2(e)(8) EXEMPTION CHALLENGE**

**LANDLORD'S CLAIM:** Property exempt from Tenant Protection Act under Civil Code 1946.2(e)(8)

**EXEMPTION REQUIREMENTS THEY MUST PROVE:**
1. **Property Type:** Single-family/duplex, alienable separate from other units
2. **Entity Type:** Cannot be REIT, corporation, or LLC with corporate member
3. **Notice Requirement:** Written exemption notice provided to tenant
4. **Timing Requirement:** If lease after July 1, 2020 = notice MUST be in rental agreement

**CHALLENGE POINTS:**
- Verify actual ownership structure (public records search)
- Demand proof of proper exemption notice
- Check if exemption notice contains exact statutory language
- Challenge property qualification (multiple units?)

**DEFENSE STRATEGY:** Exemption invalid = Full Tenant Protection Act applies

---

## **‚ö° ATTACK VECTOR #3: LIVE-IN CAREGIVER TENANT RIGHTS**

**TENANT STATUS ANALYSIS:**
- Live-in caregiver providing disability accommodation services
- California recognizes caregiver tenant rights regardless of lease status
- Fair Housing Act protections for disability-related housing
- Reasonable accommodation requirements under state/federal law

**LEGAL PROTECTIONS:**
- Cannot evict caregiver providing disability services without cause
- Must provide reasonable accommodations for disabled tenant
- Caregiver housing = protected disability accommodation
- Eviction interference with disability services = discrimination

**DEFENSE STRATEGY:** Protected tenant status + disability discrimination claim

---

## **‚ö° ATTACK VECTOR #4: LANDLORD RETALIATION - THE SMOKING GUN**

**THE KEY RETALIATION EVIDENCE:**
- Tenant attempted to rectify complaint/issue
- **LANDLORD'S EXACT WORDS:** "That's between me and them"
- **VIOLATION:** Denial of tenant's right to cure defects
- **PATTERN:** Retaliatory eviction for asserting tenant rights

**LEGAL VIOLATIONS:**
- Civil Code 1942.5: Retaliation prohibition
- Interference with tenant remedies
- Denial of due process rights
- Bad faith landlord conduct

**DEFENSE STRATEGY:** Retaliatory eviction = Case dismissal + damages

---

## **‚ö° ATTACK VECTOR #5: DUE PROCESS VIOLATIONS**

**CONSTITUTIONAL VIOLATIONS:**
- Improper service = Court lacks jurisdiction over defendant
- False sworn statements = Fraud upon the court
- Denial of right to defend = Due process violation
- Procedural violations = Void proceedings

**CUMULATIVE EFFECT:**
- Multiple procedural violations
- Pattern of landlord misconduct
- Court proceedings tainted by fraud
- Defendant denied fundamental rights

**DEFENSE STRATEGY:** Entire case void due to due process violations

---

## **üéØ DOCUMENT ANALYSIS FRAMEWORK**

**FOR EVERY DOCUMENT GROQ ANALYZES, EVALUATE:**

1. **SERVICE ISSUES:** Does this document support service defect arguments?
2. **EXEMPTION CHALLENGE:** Does this help challenge 1946.2(e)(8) exemption?

bash

# Test what files are actually in your peacock memory
python -c "
from core.database import search_all_collections
results = search_all_collections(query='a', limit=200)

print(f'üìä TOTAL RESULTS FOUND: {len(results)}')
print('=' * 60)

file_paths = set()
for i, result in enumerate(results, 1):
    metadata = result.get('metadata', {})
    file_path = metadata.get('file_path', 'No path')
    if file_path != 'No path' and not file_path.endswith('.html'):
        file_paths.add(file_path)
        if i <= 10:  # Show first 10
            print(f'{i:2d}. {file_path}')

print(f'\\nüìÅ UNIQUE FILE PATHS: {len(file_paths)}')
print('\\nüîç SAMPLE FILE PATHS:')
for i, fp in enumerate(sorted(file_paths)[:20], 1):
    print(f'{i:2d}. {fp}')
"

class ChatRequest(BaseModel):
    file_path: str
    message: str
    save_to_memory: bool = True
    selected_api_key: str = "key_1"
    context_mode: str = "fresh"  # "fresh", "resume", "summary_only"

class SummaryRequest(BaseModel):
    file_path: str
    selected_api_key: str = "key_1"

@app.get("/", response_class=HTMLResponse)

        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="war_room_fixed_layout.html not found")

    <script>
        let currentFile = null;
        let filesData = [];

        // Load file list on startup
        loadFileList();

        function getSelectedApiKey() {
            const select = document.getElementById('api-key-select');
            return select ? select.value : 'key_1';
        }

        function getContextMode() {
            const checked = document.querySelector('input[name="context-mode"]:checked');
            return checked ? checked.value : 'fresh';
        }

        async function loadFileList() {
            try {
                const response = await fetch('/api/files/status');
                const data = await response.json();
                filesData = data.files;
                renderFileList();
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Error loading files:', error);
                document.getElementById('file-list').innerHTML = '<div style="color: red;">Error loading files</div>';
            }
        }

        function renderFileList() {
            const fileList = document.getElementById('file-list');
            fileList.innerHTML = '';

            filesData.forEach((file, index) => {
                const fileDiv = document.createElement('div');
                fileDiv.className = 'file-item';
                
                fileDiv.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="file-header" onclick="toggleFileControls(${index})">
                        <div class="file-name">${file.display_name}</div>
                        <div class="file-status">
                            <div class="status-indicator ${file.has_peacock_content ? 'has-content' : ''}" title="Document Content"></div>
                            <div class="status-indicator ${file.has_chat ? 'has-chat' : ''}" title="Chat History (${file.message_count} msgs)"></div>
                            <div class="status-indicator ${file.has_summary ? 'has-summary' : ''}" title="Summary Available"></div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="file-controls" id="controls-${index}">
                        <div class="action-buttons">
                            <button class="btn primary" onclick="selectFile(${index})">Start Chat</button>
                            <button class="btn" onclick="viewFileContent('${file.file_path}', '${file.display_name}')" ${!file.has_peacock_content ? 'disabled' : ''}>View File</button>
                            <button class="btn" onclick="viewSummary('${file.file_path}')" ${!file.has_summary ? 'disabled' : ''}>View Summary</button>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                `;
                
                fileList.appendChild(fileDiv);
            });
        }

        function toggleFileControls(index) {
            const controls = document.getElementById(`controls-${index}`);
            
            document.querySelectorAll('.file-controls').forEach(ctrl => {
                if (ctrl.id !== `controls-${index}`) {
                    ctrl.classList.remove('active');
                }
            });
            
            controls.classList.toggle('active');
        }

        async function selectFile(index) {
            currentFile = filesData[index];
            
            document.getElementById('current-file').textContent = currentFile.display_name;
            document.getElementById('user-input').disabled = false;
            document.getElementById('send-btn').disabled = false;
            document.getElementById('generate-summary-btn').disabled = false;
            document.getElementById('clear-chat-btn').disabled = false;
            
            if (currentFile.has_summary) {
                document.getElementById('view-summary-btn').disabled = false;
            }

            document.getElementById(`controls-${index}`).classList.remove('active');
            
            const chatMessages = document.getElementById('chat-messages');
            chatMessages.innerHTML = `
                <div class="message assistant">
                    <div class="message-role">LEGAL WAR ROOM</div>
                    <div class="message-content">Ready to analyze: ${currentFile.display_name}

Chat Mode: ${getContextMode().toUpperCase()}
API Key: ${getSelectedApiKey()}

Using the 5 Attack Vectors framework for eviction defense.</div>
                </div>
            `;
            
            document.getElementById('user-input').focus();
        }

        async function sendMessage() {
            if (!currentFile) return;

            const userInput = document.getElementById('user-input');
            const message = userInput.value.trim();
            if (!message) return;

            addMessage('user', message);
            userInput.value = '';

            const saveMemory = document.getElementById('save-memory').checked;
            const selectedKey = getSelectedApiKey();
            const contextMode = getContextMode();

            try {
                const response = await fetch('/api/chat', {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: {
                        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                    },
                    body: JSON.stringify({
                        file_path: currentFile.file_path,
                        message: message,
                        save_to_memory: saveMemory,
                        selected_api_key: selectedKey,
                        context_mode: contextMode
                    })
                });

                const data = await response.json();
                addMessage('assistant', data.response);

                if (data.saved_to_memory) {
                    await loadFileList();
                }
            } catch (error) {
                addMessage('assistant', 'Error: Failed to get response from AI.');
                console.error('Chat error:', error);
            }
        }

        function addMessage(role, content) {
            const chatMessages = document.getElementById('chat-messages');
            const messageDiv = document.createElement('div');
            messageDiv.className = `message ${role}`;
            
            messageDiv.innerHTML = `
                <div class="message-role">${role.toUpperCase()}</div>
                <div class="message-content">${content}</div>
            `;
            
            chatMessages.appendChild(messageDiv);
            chatMessages.scrollTop = chatMessages.scrollHeight;
        }

        async function generateSummary() {
            if (!currentFile) return;
            
            const selectedKey = getSelectedApiKey();

            try {
                const response = await fetch('/api/generate-summary', {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: {
                        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                    },
                    body: JSON.stringify({
                        file_path: currentFile.file_path,
                        selected_api_key: selectedKey
                    })
                });

                const data = await response.json();
                
                document.getElementById('summary-modal-title').textContent = `Summary: ${currentFile.display_name}`;
                document.getElementById('summary-modal-content').innerHTML = `<pre>${data.summary}</pre>`;
                document.getElementById('summary-modal').style.display = 'block';

                await loadFileList();
                document.getElementById('view-summary-btn').disabled = false;
            } catch (error) {
                alert('Error generating summary: ' + error.message);
            }
        }

        async function viewSummary(filePath) {
            try {
                const response = await fetch(`/api/summary/${encodeURIComponent(filePath)}`);
                const data = await response.json();
                
                document.getElementById('summary-modal-title').textContent = `Summary: ${filePath}`;
                document.getElementById('summary-modal-content').innerHTML = `<pre>${data.summary}</pre>`;
                document.getElementById('summary-modal').style.display = 'block';
            } catch (error) {
                alert('Error loading summary: ' + error.message);
            }
        }

        async function viewFileContent(filePath, displayName) {
            document.getElementById('modal-title').textContent = displayName;
            document.getElementById('modal-content').innerHTML = '<div>Loading file content...</div>';
            document.getElementById('file-modal').style.display = 'block';
            
            // Load actual file content from peacock memory
            try {
                // This would be enhanced to actually fetch file content
                document.getElementById('modal-content').innerHTML = `<pre>File: ${filePath}

This is



-----------------------------------

I NEED YOU TO FIX THIS SHIT. 

1 LAST FUCKING TIME MAKE IT FUCKING BAD ASS YOU HAVE ALL THE INFO U NEED TO MAKE THIS go!! 



    Modular Command Architecture: Every command is a self-contained module. One piece fails, the rest of the operation keeps running. That's smart engineering. (commands/ directory)

    Project-Based Organization: You can wall off different hustles. The eviction_defense project keeps all its code, notes, and strategy docs separate from your global intel. (commands/project_handler.py)

    Smart Importers: The system automatically recognizes and assimilates intel from Claude and ChatGPT conversation exports, getting it into the database fast. (core/importers.py)

    File Disposition System: Every piece of data gets tagged: Codebase, Plan/Brainstorm, Idea, Note, or man-page. This allows for surgical strikes when you're searching.

Command & Control (The User Interface)

    Interactive CLI: This ain't your grandaddy's command line. It's a dynamic, menu-driven interface powered by questionary, guiding you through every play.

    Dedicated War Room Window (No Browser Bullshit): Your War Room UI launches in its own dedicated, chromeless window using pywebview. No address bar, no bookmarks, no distractions. Just a pure, professional command center. (run_war_room.py)

    Cyberpunk Visuals: The system has style. 80+ unique cfonts banners, random ornate borders, and a neon color palette make it look like something straight outta a digital hustle. (core/visuals.py)

    Power-User File Handling: Add single files or whole directories. It even uses fzf for a lightning-fast, interactive file-picker if you got it installed. (commands/file_handler.py)

    Comprehensive Deletion: A full interactive delete menu with multiple safety levels, from sniping a single file to a "nuclear option" to wipe the slate clean, with confirmations at every critical step. (commands/delete_handler.py)

External System Integration (The Connect)

    Proper MCP Integration: Connects to Claude Desktop the right way‚ÄîJSON-RPC over stdio. No janky HTTP workarounds. This is the official, stable protocol. (mcp_server_proper.py)

    One-Command Claude Setup: The mcp-config command is a G move. It finds your Claude Desktop config, backs it up, and writes the new settings to perfectly integrate your custom tools. Zero friction. (commands/mcp_config_handler.py)

    Local LLM War Room: You have an ollama_handler to jack into your own private, local LLM, keeping your most sensitive analysis off-grid.

    Multi-Step Groq Orchestrator: This ain't just a simple prompt. Your groq_function_caller.py runs a sophisticated chain: it uses a powerful model to search for intel, plan its analysis, execute by reading specific file chunks, and then synthesize a final answer. High-level AI strategy.


    Per-File Session Memory: The ConversationManager is your ledger, tracking every chat and summary tied to a specific legal file. This lets you go deep on one piece of evidence without cross-contamination.

    Legal Content Bulk Loader: A dedicated script to ingest your entire legal research library into the eviction_defense project, tagging it and getting it ready for the fight. (legal_content_loader.py)

            document.getElementById('modal-title').textContent = displayName;\

            modalBody.textContent = 'Loading...';\
            document.getElementById('file-modal').style.display = 'block';\
            try {\
                const response = await fetch(\`/api/document/\${encodeURIComponent(filePath)}\`);\
                if (!response.ok) throw new Error(\`Server responded with \${response.status}\`);\
                const data = await response.json();\

            } catch (error) { modalBody.textContent = 'Error loading file content: ' + error.message; }\

@app.get(\"/api/document/{file_path:path}\", tags=[\"Document\"])\
def get_document_content(file_path: str):\
    print(f\"\\n[DOC LOG] Fetching content for: {file_path}\")\
    results = search_all_collections(query=file_path.replace('.md', ''), limit=5)\
    for result in results:\
        metadata = result.get('metadata', {})\
        if file_path == metadata.get('file_path', ''):\
            return PlainTextResponse(content=result.get('document', ''))\
    raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=\"Document content not found\")" mcp_api_bridge_ultimate.py
